a style, useful for clearing regions before popups\n+\n+const std = @import(\"std\");\n+const buffer_mod = @import(\"../buffer.zig\");\n+const geometry = @import(\"../geometry.zig\");\n+const style_mod = @import(\"../style.zig\");\n+\n+pub const Buffer = buffer_mod.Buffer;\n+pub const Cell = buffer_mod.Cell;\n+pub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\n+pub const Style = style_mod.Style;\n+\n+/// Clear widget that fills an area with a style.\n+///\n+/// Useful for:\n+/// - Clearing a region before rendering a popup or overlay\n+/// - Drawing a solid background area\n+/// - Erasing content in a specific region\n+pub const Clear = struct {\n+    /// Style to fill the area with.\n+    /// The background color of this style determines the fill color.\n+    style: Style = Style.empty,\n+\n+    /// Character to fill with. Defaults to space.\n+    char: u21 = ' ',\n+\n+    /// Render the clear widget into the buffer at the given area.\n+    /// Fills the entire area with the style and character.\n+    pub fn render(self: Clear, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n+        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n+\n+        const fill_cell = Cell.styled(self.char, self.style);\n+        buf.fill(area, fill_cell);\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Create a clear widget with a background color.\n+    pub fn withBackground(color: style_mod.Color) Clear {\n+        return .{\n+            .style = Style.init().bg(color),\n+        };\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// SANITY TESTS - Basic Clear functionality\n+// 0000000..e7fc2df\n--- /dev/null\n+++ b/src/widgets/scrollbar.zig\n@@ -0,0 +1,408 @@\n+// Scrollbar widget for zithril TUI framework\n+// Scroll position indicator with configurable orientation and style\n+\n+const std = @import(\"std\");\n+const buffer_mod = @import(\"../buffer.zig\");\n+const geometry = @import(\"../geometry.zig\");\n+const style_mod = @import(\"../style.zig\");\n+\n+pub const Buffer = buffer_mod.Buffer;\n+pub const Cell = buffer_mod.Cell;\n+pub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\n+pub const Style = style_mod.Style;\n+\n+/// Scrollbar orientation.\n+pub const Orientation = enum {\n+    vertical,\n+    horizontal,\n+};\n+\n+/// Scroll position indicator widget.\n+///\n+/// Displays a scrollbar track with a thumb indicating the current scroll position.\n+/// The thumb size is proportional to the viewport size relative to total content.\n+/// Supports both vertical and horizontal orientations.\n+pub const Scrollbar = struct {\n+    /// Total number of items/lines in the scrollable content.\n+    total: usize = 0,\n+\n+    /// Current scroll position (index of first visible item).\n+    position: usize = 0,\n+\n+    /// Number of items visible in the viewport.\n+    viewport: u16 = 0,\n+\n+    /// Style applied to the scrollbar track.\n+    style: Style = Style.empty,\n+\n+    /// Style applied to the scrollbar thumb.\n+    thumb_style: Style = Style.init().reverse(),\n+\n+    /// Orientation of the scrollbar.\n+    orientation: Orientation = .vertical,\n+\n+    /// Characters used for rendering.\n+    /// Track character fills the scrollbar background.\n+    track_char: u21 = ' ',\n+\n+    /// Thumb character fills the scrollbar thumb.\n+    thumb_char: u21 = ' ',\n+\n+    /// Render the scrollbar into the buffer at the given area.\n+    pub fn render(self: Scrollbar, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n+        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n+\n+        const track_length = switch (self.orientation) {\n+            .vertical => area.height,\n+            .horizontal => area.width,\n+        };\n+\n+        if (track_length == 0) return;\n+\n+        // Draw the track first\n+        self.drawTrack(area, buf);\n+\n+        // Calculate and draw the thumb\n+        if (self.total > 0 and self.viewport > 0) {\n+            const thumb_info = self.calculateThumb(track_length);\n+            self.drawThumb(area, thumb_info.start, thumb_info.length, buf);\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Draw the scrollbar track.\n+    fn drawTrack(self: Scrollbar, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n+        const track_cell = Cell.styled(self.track_char, self.style);\n+\n+        switch (self.orientation) {\n+            .vertical => {\n+                var y = area.y;\n+                while (y < area.bottom()) : (y += 1) {\n+                    buf.set(area.x, y, track_cell);\n+                }\n+            },\n+            .horizontal => {\n+                var x = area.x;\n+                while (x < area.right()) : (x += 1) {\n+                    buf.set(x, area.y, track_cell);\n+                }\n+            },\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Draw the scrollbar thumb at the calculated position.\n+    fn drawThumb(self: Scrollbar, area: Rect, start: u16, length: u16, buf: *Buffer) void {\n+        if (length == 0) return;\n+\n+        const thumb_cell = Cell.styled(self.thumb_char, self.thumb_style);\n+\n+        switch (self.orientation) {\n+            .vertical => {\n+                const thumb_y = area.y +| start;\n+                var y = thumb_y;\n+                while (y < thumb_y +| length and y < area.bottom()) : (y += 1) {\n+                    buf.set(area.x, y, thumb_cell);\n+                }\n+            },\n+            .horizontal => {\n+                const thumb_x = area.x +| start;\n+                var x = thumb_x;\n+                while (x < thumb_x +| length and x < area.right()) : (x += 1) {\n+                    buf.set(x, area.y, thumb_cell);\n+                }\n+            },\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Calculate thumb position and size.\n+    fn calculateThumb(self: Scrollbar, track_length: u16) struct { start: u16, length: u16 } {\n+        if (self.total == 0 or self.viewport == 0 or track_length == 0) {\n+            return .{ .start = 0, .length = 0 };\n+        }\n+\n+        const total_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(self.total);\n+        const viewport_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(self.viewport);\n+        const track_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(track_length);\n+        const position_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(self.position);\n+\n+        // Thumb length proportional to viewport/total ratio\n+        const thumb_ratio = @min(viewport_f / total_f, 1.0);\n+        var thumb_length: u16 = @intFromFloat(@max(thumb_ratio * track_f, 1.0));\n+        thumb_length = @min(thumb_length, track_length);\n+\n+        // Thumb position based on scroll position\n+        const scrollable_items = if (self.total > self.viewport)\n+            self.total - self.viewport\n+        else\n+            0;\n+\n+        var thumb_start: u16 = 0;\n+        if (scrollable_items > 0) {\n+            const scrollable_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(scrollable_items);\n+            const scrollable_track = track_length -| thumb_length;\n+            const scrollable_track_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(scrollable_track);\n+\n+            const position_ratio = @min(position_f / scrollable_f, 1.0);\n+            thumb_start = @intFromFloat(position_ratio * scrollable_track_f);\n+        }\n+\n+        return .{ .start = thumb_start, .length = thumb_length };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Create a scrollbar for a list with the given state.\n+    pub fn forList(items_count: usize, selected: usize, visible_rows: u16) Scrollbar {\n+        return .{\n+            .total = items_count,\n+            .position = selected,\n+            .viewport = visible_rows,\n+        };\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// SANITY TESTS - Basic Scrollbar functionality\n+// ============================================================\n+\n+test \"sanity: Scrollbar with default values\" {\n+    const scrollbar = Scrollbar{};\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), scrollbar.total);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), scrollbar.position);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 0), scrollbar.viewport);\n+    try std.testing.expect(scrollbar.orientation == .vertical);\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: Scrollbar with values\" {\n+    const scrollbar = Scrollbar{\n+        .total = 100,\n+        .position = 25,\n+        .viewport = 10,\n+        .orientation = .horizontal,\n+    };\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 100), scrollbar.total);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 25), scrollbar.position);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 10), scrollbar.viewport);\n+    try std.testing.expect(scrollbar.orientation == .horizontal);\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: Scrollbar.forList creates correctly\" {\n+    const scrollbar = Scrollbar.forList(50, 10, 20);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 50), scrollbar.total);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 10), scrollbar.position);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 20), scrollbar.viewport);\n+}\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// BEHAVIOR TESTS - Rendering\n+// ============================================================\n+\n+test \"behavior: Scrollbar renders vertical track\" {\n+    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 10, 10);\n+    defer buf.deinit();\n+\n+    const scrollbar = Scrollbar{\n+        .total = 100,\n+        .position = 0,\n+        .viewport = 10,\n+        .style = Style.init().bg(.blue),\n+    };\n+    scrollbar.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 1, 10), &buf);\n+\n+    // Track should be drawn along the height\n+    const cell = buf.get(0, 5);\n+    try std.testing.expect(cell.style.getBackground() != null);\n+}\n+\n+test \"behavior: Scrollbar renders horizontal track\" {\n+    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 5);\n+    defer buf.deinit();\n+\n+    const scrollbar = Scrollbar{\n+        .total = 100,\n+        .position = 0,\n+        .viewport = 10,\n+        .orientation = .horizontal,\n+        .style = Style.init().bg(.blue),\n+    };\n+    scrollbar.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 20, 1), &buf);\n+\n+    // Track should be drawn along the width\n+    const cell = buf.get(10, 0);\n+    try std.testing.expect(cell.style.getBackground() != {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_015hyvCVaHiZ6ZonmhdB2zhD","type":"tool_result","content":"     1// Paragraph widget for zithril TUI framework\n     2// Multi-line text with wrapping and alignment\n     3\n     4const std = @import(\"std\");\n     5const buffer_mod = @import(\"../buffer.zig\");\n     6const geometry = @import(\"../geometry.zig\");\n     7const style_mod = @import(\"../style.zig\");\n     8const text_mod = @import(\"../text.zig\");\n     9\n    10pub const Buffer = buffer_mod.Buffer;\n    11pub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\n    12pub const Style = style_mod.Style;\n    13\n    14/// Text wrapping modes\n    15pub const Wrap = enum {\n    16    /// No wrapping, clip at boundary\n    17    none,\n    18    /// Wrap at any character position\n    19    char,\n    20    /// Wrap at word boundaries (spaces)\n    21    word,\n    22};\n    23\n    24/// Text alignment options\n    25pub const Alignment = enum {\n    26    left,\n    27    center,\n    28    right,\n    29};\n    30\n    31/// Multi-line text widget with optional wrapping.\n    32///\n    33/// Renders text content across multiple lines with configurable wrapping\n    34/// behavior and alignment. Lines beyond the area height are not rendered.\n    35pub const Paragraph = struct {\n    36    /// The text content to display\n    37    text: []const u8,\n    38\n    39    /// Style applied to the text\n    40    style: Style = Style.empty,\n    41\n    42    /// Text wrapping mode\n    43    wrap: Wrap = .none,\n    44\n    45    /// Text alignment within each line\n    46    alignment: Alignment = .left,\n    47\n    48    /// Render the paragraph into the buffer at the given area.\n    49    /// Text is split into lines (either by newlines or wrapping) and rendered\n    50    /// until the area height is filled.\n    51    pub fn render(self: Paragraph, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n    52        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n    53        if (self.text.len == 0) return;\n    54\n    55        var y = area.y;\n    56        const max_y = area.bottom();\n    57\n    58        // Process text line by line (split by newlines first)\n    59        var line_iter = std.mem.splitScalar(u8, self.text, '\\n');\n    60        while (line_iter.next()) |logical_line| {\n    61            if (y >= max_y) break;\n    62\n    63            // Apply wrapping to this logical line\n    64            switch (self.wrap) {\n    65                .none => {\n    66                    self.renderLine(logical_line, area.x, y, area.width, buf);\n    67                    y += 1;\n    68                },\n    69                .char => {\n    70                    var remaining = logical_line;\n    71                    while (remaining.len > 0 and y < max_y) {\n    72                        const chunk_len = @min(remaining.len, area.width);\n    73                        const chunk = remaining[0..chunk_len];\n    74                        self.renderLine(chunk, area.x, y, area.width, buf);\n    75                        remaining = remaining[chunk_len..];\n    76                        y += 1;\n    77                    }\n    78                    // Empty line should still take a row\n    79                    if (logical_line.len == 0) {\n    80                        y += 1;\n    81                    }\n    82                },\n    83                .word => {\n    84                    if (logical_line.len == 0) {\n    85                        y += 1;\n    86                        continue;\n    87                    }\n    88                    var line_start: usize = 0;\n    89                    while (line_start < logical_line.len and y < max_y) {\n    90                        const wrap_end = findWordWrapEnd(logical_line[line_start..], area.width);\n    91                        const line = logical_line[line_start .. line_start + wrap_end];\n    92                        self.renderLine(line, area.x, y, area.width, buf);\n    93                        line_start += wrap_end;\n    94                        // Skip leading spaces on next line\n    95                        while (line_start < logical_line.len and logical_line[line_start] == ' ') {\n    96                            line_start += 1;\n    97                        }\n    98                        y += 1;\n    99                    }\n   100                },\n   101            }\n   102        }\n   103    }\n   104\n   105    /// Render a single line of text with alignment\n   106    fn renderLine(self: Paragraph, line: []const u8, x: u16, y: u16, width: u16, buf: *Buffer) void {\n   107        if (line.len == 0) return;\n   108\n   109        const text_len = text_mod.displayWidth(line);\n   110        const visible_len = @min(text_len, width);\n   111\n   112        if (visible_len == 0) return;\n   113\n   114        const x_offset: u16 = switch (self.alignment) {\n   115            .left => 0,\n   116            .center => (width -| visible_len) / 2,\n   117            .right => width -| visible_len,\n   118        };\n   119\n   120        buf.setString(x +| x_offset, y, line, self.style);\n   121    }\n   122};\n   123\n   124/// Find the end index for word wrapping within a max width.\n   125/// Returns the number of characters to include on this line.\n   126fn findWordWrapEnd(text: []const u8, max_width: u16) usize {\n   127    if (text.len == 0) return 0;\n   128\n   129    const width: usize = @intCast(max_width);\n   130    if (text.len <= width) return text.len;\n   131\n   132    // Find the last space within the width limit\n   133    var last_space: ?usize = null;\n   134    for (0..width) |i| {\n   135        if (text[i] == ' ') {\n   136            last_space = i;\n   137        }\n   138    }\n   139\n   140    // If we found a space, wrap there (include the space in this line)\n   141    if (last_space) |space_pos| {\n   142        // Return position including the space, so next line starts after it\n   143        return space_pos + 1;\n   144    }\n   145\n   146    // No space found - break at max width (hard wrap)\n   147    return width;\n   148}\n   149\n   150// ============================================================\n   151// SANITY TESTS - Basic Paragraph functionality\n   152// ============================================================\n   153\n   154test \"sanity: Paragraph with default values\" {\n   155    const para = Paragraph{ .text = \"Hello\\nWorld\" };\n   156    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"Hello\\nWorld\", para.text);\n   157    try std.testing.expect(para.style.isEmpty());\n   158    try std.testing.expect(para.wrap == .none);\n   159    try std.testing.expect(para.alignment == .left);\n   160}\n   161\n   162test \"sanity: Paragraph with custom style\" {\n   163    const para = Paragraph{\n   164        .text = \"Styled\",\n   165 const none_wrap = Paragraph{ .text = \"T\", .wrap = .none };\n   172    const char_wrap = Paragraph{ .text = \"T\", .wrap = .char };\n   173    const word_wrap = Paragraph{ .text = \"T\", .wrap = .word };\n   174\n   175    try std.testing.expect(none_wrap.wrap == .none);\n   176    try std.testing.expect(char_wrap.wrap == .char);\n   177    try std.testing.expect(word_wrap.wrap == .word);\n   178}\n   179\n   180test \"sanity: Paragraph with alignment\" {\n   181    const left = Paragraph{ .text = \"L\", .alignment = .left };\n   182    const center = Paragraph{ .text = \"C\", .alignment = .center };\n   183    const right = Paragraph{ .text = \"R\", .alignment = .right };\n   184\n   185    try std.testing.expect(left.alignment == .left);\n   186    try std.testing.expect(center.alignment == .center);\n   187    try std.testing.expect(right.alignment == .right);\n   188}\n   189\n   190// ============================================================\n Lines beyond the area height are not rendered.\npub const Paragraph = struct {\n    /// The text content to display\n    text: []const u8,\n\n    /// Style applied to the text\n    style: Style = Style.empty,\n\n    /// Text wrapping mode\n    wrap: Wrap = .none,\n\n    /// Text alignment within each line\n    alignment: Alignment = .left,\n\n    /// Render the paragraph into the buffer at the given area.\n    /// Text is split into lines (either by newlines or wrapping) and rendered\n    /// until the area height is filled.\n    pub fn render(self: Paragraph, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n        if (self.text.len == 0) return;\n\n        var y = area.y;\n        const max_y = area.bottom();\n\n        // Process text line by line (split by newlines first)\n        var line_iter = std.mem.splitScalar(u8, self.text, '\\n');\n        while (line_iter.next()) |logical_line| {\n            if (y >= max_y) break;\n\n            // Apply wrapping to this logical line\n            switch (self.wrap) {\n                .none => {\n                    self.renderLine(logical_line, area.x, y, area.width, buf);\n                    y += 1;\n                },\n                .char => {\n                    var remaining = logical_line;\n                    while (remaining.len > 0 and y < max_y) {\n                        const chunk_len = @min(remaining.len, area.width);\n                        const chunk = remaining[0..chunk_len];\n                        self.renderLine(chunk, area.x, y, area.width, buf);\n                        remaining = remaining[chunk_len..];\n                        y += 1;\n                    }\n                    // Empty line should still take a row\n                    if (logical_line.len == 0) {\n                        y += 1;\n                    }\n                },\n                .word => {\n                    if (logical_line.len == 0) {\n                        y += 1;\n                        continue;\n                    }\n                    var line_start: usize = 0;\n                    while (line_start < logical_line.len and y < max_y) {\n                        const wrap_end = findWordWrapEnd(logical_line[line_start..], area.width);\n                        const line = logical_line[line_start .. line_start + wrap_end];\n                        self.renderLine(line, area.x, y, area.width, buf);\n                        line_start += wrap_end;\n                        // Skip leading spaces on next line\n                        while (line_start < logical_line.len and logical_line[line_start] == ' ') {\n                            line_start += 1;\n                        }\n                        y += 1;\n                    }\n                },\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Render a single line of text with alignment\n    fn renderLine(self: Paragraph, line: []const u8, x: u16, y: u16, width: u16, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        if (line.len == 0) return;\n\n        const text_len = text_mod.displayWidth(line);\n        const visible_len = @min(text_len, width);\n\n        if (visible_len == 0) return;\n\n        const x_offset: u16 = switch (self.alignment) {\n            .left => 0,\n            .center => (width -| visible_len) / 2,\n            .right => width -| visible_len,\n        };\n\n        buf.setString(x +| x_offset, y, line, self.style);\n    }\n};\n\n/// Find the end index for word wrapping within a max width.\n/// Returns the number of characters to include on this line.\nfn findWordWrapEnd(text: []const u8, max_width: u16) usize {\n    if (text.len == 0) return 0;\n\n    const width: usize = @intCast(max_width);\n    if (text.len <= width) return text.len;\n\n    // Find the last space within the width limit\n    var last_space: ?usize = null;\n    for (0..width) |i| {\n        if (text[i] == ' ') {\n            last_space = i;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // If we found a space, wrap there (include the space in this line)\n    if (last_space) |space_pos| {\n        // Return position including the space, so next line starts after it\n        return space_pos + 1;\n    }\n\n    // No space found - break at max width (hard wrap)\n    return width;\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// SANITY TESTS - Basic Paragraph functionality\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"sanity: Paragraph with default values\" {\n    const para = Paragraph{ .text = \"Hello\\nWorld\" };\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"Hello\\nWorld\", para.text);\n    try std.testing.expect(para.style.isEmpty());\n    try std.testing.expect(para.wrap == .none);\n    try std.testing.expect(para.alignment == .left);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: Paragraph with custom style\" {\n    const para = Paragraph{\n        .text = \"Styled\",\n        .style = Style.init().bold().fg(.red),\n    };\n    try std.testing.expect(para.style.hasAttribute(.bold));\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: Paragraph with wrap modes\" {\n    const none_wrap = Paragraph{ .text = \"T\", .wrap = .none };\n    const char_wrap = Paragraph{ .text = \"T\", .wrap = .char };\n    const word_wrap = Paragraph{ .text = \"T\", .wrap = .word };\n\n    try std.testing.expect(none_wrap.wrap == .none);\n    try std.testing.expect(char_wrap.wrap == .char);\n    try std.testing.expect(word_wrap.wrap == .word);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: Paragraph with alignment\" {\n    const left = Paragraph{ .text = \"L\", .alignment = .left };\n    const center = Paragraph{ .text = \"C\", .alignment = .center };\n    const right = Paragraph{ .text = \"R\", .alignment = .right };\n\n    try std.testing.expect(left.alignment == .left);\n    try std.testing.expect(center.alignment == .center);\n    try std.testing.expect(right.alignment == .right);\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// BEHAVIOR TESTS - Rendering\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"behavior: Paragraph renders single line\" {\n    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 5);\n    defer buf.deinit();\n\n    const para = Paragraph{ .text = \"Hello\" };\n    para.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 20, 5), &buf);\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'H'), buf.get(0, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'e'), buf.get(1, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'l'), buf.get(2, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'l'), buf.get(3, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'o'), buf.get(4, 0).char);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: Paragraph renders multiple lines with newlines\" {\n    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 5);\n    defer buf.deinit();\n\n    const para = Paragraph{ .text = \"Line1\\nLine2\\nLine3\" };\n    para.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 20, 5), &buf);\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'L'), buf.get(0, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, '1'), buf.get(4, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'L'), buf.get(0, 1).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, '2'), buf.get(4, 1).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'L'), buf.get(0, 2).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, '3'), buf.get(4, 2).char);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: Paragraph with char wrap\" {\n    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 10, 5);\n    defer buf.deinit();\n\n    const para = Paragraph{\n        .text = \"ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOP\",\n        .wrap = .char,\n    };\n    para.render(Rect.init(0, 0, 10, 5), &buf);\n\n    // First 10 chars on row 0\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'A'), buf.get(0, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'J'), buf.get(9, 0).char);\n    // Next 6 chars on row 1\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'K'), buf.get(0, 1).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'P'), buf.get(5, 1).char);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: Paragraph with word wrap\" {\n    var buf = try 0, 10, 5), &buf);\n\n    // \"Hello \" should be on row 0\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'H'), buf.get(0, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'o'), buf.get(4, 0).char);\n    // \"World \" should be on row 1\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'W'), buf.get(0, 1).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'd'), buf.get(4, 1).char);\n    // \"Today\" should be on row 2\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'T'), buf.get(0, 2).char);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: Paragraph center alignment\" {\n    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 20, 5);\n in 20 = offset 9\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'H'), buf.get(9, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'i'), buf.get(10, 0).char);\n}\n\ntest \"behavior: Paragraph right // Only first 2 lines should be rendered\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, 'L'), buf.get(0, 0).char);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u21, '1'), buf.get(4, 0).char);\n    try @import(\"../geometry.zig\");\nconst style_mod = @import(\"../style.zig\");\nconst text_mod = @import(\"../text.zig\");\n\npub const Buffer = buffer_mod.Buffer;\npub const Cell = buffer_mod.Cell;\npub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\npub const Style = style_mod.Style;\n\n/// Tabs widget displaying a horizontal tab bar.\n///\n/// Renders a row of tab titles with the selected tab highlighted.\n/// Tabs are separated by a configurable divider string.\npub const Tabs = struct {\n    /// Tab titles to display\n    titles: []const []const u8,\n\n    /// Index of the currently selected tab\n    selected: usize = 0,\n\n    /// Default style for unselected tabs\n    style: Style = Style.empty,\n\n    /// Style for the selected tab\n    highlight_style: Style = Style.init().bold().fg(.yellow),\n\n    /// Divider string between tabs\n    divider: []const u8 = \" | \",\n\n    /// Render the tabs into the buffer at the given area.\n    /// Tabs are rendered horizontally on the first row of the area.\n    pub fn render(self: Tabs, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n        if (self.titles.len == 0) return;\n\n        var x = area.x;\n\n        for (self.titles, 0..) |title, idx| {\n            if (x >= area.right()) break;\n\n            // Determine if this tab is selected\n            const is_selected = idx == self.selected;\n            const tab_style = if (is_selected) self.highlight_style else self.style;\n\n            // Render tab title\n            const available_width = area.right() -| x;\n            if (available_width == 0) break;\n\n            const title_len = text_mod.displayWidth(title);\n            const render_len = @min(title_len, available_width);\n\n            if (render_len > 0) {\n                buf.setString(x, area.y, title, tab_style);\n            }\n\n            x +|= @intCast(render_len);\n\n            // Render divider after tab (except for last tab)\n            if (idx + 1 < self.titles.len and x < area.right()) {\n                const divider_available = area.right() -| x;\n                const divider_len = text_mod.displayWidth(self.divider);\n                const divider_render_len = @min(divider_len, divider_available);\n\n                if (divider_render_len > 0) {\n                    buf.setString(x, area.y, self.divider, self.style);\n                }\n\n                x +|= @intCast(divider_render_len);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Get the number of tabs\n    pub fn count(self: Tabs) usize {\n        return self.titles.len;\n    }\n\n    /// Check if tabs are empty\n    pub fn isEmpty(self: Tabs) bool {\n        return self.titles.len == 0;\n    }\n\n    /// Get the selected tab index, clamped to valid range\n    pub fn selectedClamped(self: Tabs) ?usize {\n        if (self.titles.len == 0) return null;\n        return @min(self.selected, self.titles.len - 1);\n    }\n};\n\n// ============================================================\n//    20/// Scroll position indicator widget.\n    21///\n    22/// Displays a scrollbar track with a thumb indicating the current scroll position.\n    23/// The thumb size is proportional to the viewport size relative to total content.\n    24/// Supports both vertical and horizontal orientations.\n    25pub const Scrollbar = struct {\n    26    /// Total number of items/lines in the scrollable content.\n    27    total: usize = 0,\n    28\n    29    /// Current scroll position (index of first visible item).\n    30    position: usize = 0,\n    31\n    32    /// Number of items scrollbar thumb.\n    39    thumb_style: Style = Style.init().reverse(),\n    40\n    41    /// Orientation of the scrollbar.\n    42    orientation: Orientation = .vertical,\n    43\n    44    /// Characters used for rendering.\n    45    /// Track character fills the scrollbar background.\n    46    track_char: u21 = ' ',\n    47\n    48    /// Thumb character fills the scrollbar thumb.\n    49    thumb_char: u21 = ' ',\n    50\n    51    /// Render the scrollbar into the buffer at the given area.\n    52    pub fn render(self: Scrollbar, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n    53        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n    54\n    55        const track_length = switch (self.orientation) {\n    56            .vertical => area.height,\n    57            .horizontal => area.width,\n    58        };\n    59\n    60        if (track_length == 0) return;\n    61\n    62        // Draw the track first\n    63        self.drawTrack(area, buf);\n    64\n    65        // Calculate and draw the thumb\n    66        if (self.total > 0 and self.viewport > 0) {\n    67            const thumb_info = self.calculateThumb(track_length);\n    68            self.drawThumb(area, thumb_info.start, thumb_info.length, buf);\n    69        }\n    70    }\n    71\n    72    /// Draw the scrollbar track.\n    73    fn drawTrack(self: Scrollbar, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n    74        const track_cell = Cell.styled(self.track_char, self.style);\n    75\n    76        switch (self.orientation) {\n    77            .vertical => {\n    78                var y = area.y;\n    79                while (y < area.bottom()) : (y += 1) {\n    80                    buf.set(area.x, y, track_cell);\n    81                }\n    82            },\n    83            .horizontal => {\n    84                var x = area.x;\n    85                while (x < area.right()) : (x += 1) {\n    86                    buf.set(x, area.y, track_cell);\n    87                }\n    88            },\n    89        }\n    90    }\n    91\n    92    /// Draw the scrollbar thumb at the calculated position.\n    93    fn drawThumb(self: Scrollbar, area: Rect, start: u16, length: u16, buf: *Buffer) void {\n    94        if (length == 0) return;\n    95\n    96        const thumb_cell = Cell.styled(self.thumb_char, self.thumb_style);\n    97\n    98        switch (self.orientation) {\n    99            .vertical 112            },\n   113        }\n   114    }\n   115\n   116    /// Calculate thumb position and size.\n   117    fn calculateThumb(self: Scrollbar, track_length: u16) struct { start: u16, length: u16 } {\n   118        if (self.total == 0 or self.viewport == 0 or track_length == 0) {\n   119            return .{ .start = 0, .length = 0 };\n   120        }\n   121\n   122        const total_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(self.position);\n   126\n   127        // Thumb length proportional to viewport/total ratio\n   128        const thumb_ratio = @min(viewport_f / total_f, 1.0);\n   129        var thumb_length: u16 = @intFromFloat(@max(thumb_ratio * track_f, 1.0));\n   130        thumb_length = @min(thumb_length, track_length);\n   131\n   132        // Thumb position based on scroll position\n   133        const scrollable_items = if (self.total > self.viewport)\n   134            self.total - self.viewport\n   135        else\n   136            0;\n   137\n   138        var thumb_start: u16 = 0;\n   139        if (scrollable_items > 0) {\n   140            const scrollable_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(scrollable_items);\n   141            const scrollable_track = track_length -| thumb_length;\n   142            const scrollable_track_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(scrollable_track);\n   143\n   144            const position_ratio = @min(position_f / scrollable_f, 1.0);\n   145            thumb_start = @intFromFloat(position_ratio * scrollable_track_f);\n   146        }\n   147\n   148        return .{ .start = thumb_start, .length = thumb_length };\n   149    }\n   150\n   151    /// Create a scrollbar for a list with the given state.\n   152    pub fn forList(items_count: usize, selected: usize, visible_rows: u16) Scrollbar {\n   153        return .{\n   154            .total Scrollbar widget for zithril TUI framework\n// Scroll position indicator with configurable orientation and style\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst buffer_mod = @import(\"../buffer.zig\");\nconst geometry = @import(\"../geometry.zig\");\nconst style_mod = @import(\"../style.zig\");\n\npub const Buffer = buffer_mod.Buffer;\npub const Cell = buffer_mod.Cell;\npub const Rect = geometry.Rect;\npub const Style = style_mod.Style;\n\n/// Scrollbar orientation.\npub const Orientation = enum {\n    vertical,\n    horizontal,\n};\n\n/// Scroll position indicator widget.\n///\n/// Displays a scrollbar track with a thumb indicating the current scroll position.\n/// The thumb size is proportional to the viewport size relative to total content.\n/// Supports both vertical and horizontal orientations.\npub const Scrollbar = struct {\n    /// Total number of items/lines in the scrollable content.\n    total: usize = 0,\n\n    /// Current scroll position (index of first visible item).\n    position: usize = 0,\n\n    /// Number of items visible in the viewport.\n    viewport: u16 = 0,\n\n    /// Style applied to the scrollbar track.\n    style: Style = Style.empty,\n\n    /// Style applied to the scrollbar thumb.\n    thumb_style: Style = Style.init().reverse(),\n\n    /// Orientation of the scrollbar.\n    orientation: Orientation = .vertical,\n\n    /// Characters used for rendering.\n    /// Track character fills the scrollbar background.\n    track_char: u21 = ' ',\n\n    /// Thumb character fills the scrollbar thumb.\n    thumb_char: u21 = ' ',\n\n    /// Render the scrollbar into the buffer at the given area.\n    pub fn render(self: Scrollbar, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        if (area.isEmpty()) return;\n\n        const track_length = switch (self.orientation) {\n            .vertical => area.height,\n            .horizontal => area.width,\n        };\n\n        if (track_length == 0) return;\n\n        // Draw the track first\n        self.drawTrack(area, buf);\n\n        // Calculate and draw the thumb\n        if (self.total > 0 and self.viewport > 0) {\n            const thumb_info = self.calculateThumb(track_length);\n            self.drawThumb(area, thumb_info.start, thumb_info.length, buf);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Draw the scrollbar track.\n    fn drawTrack(self: Scrollbar, area: Rect, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        const track_cell = Cell.styled(self.track_char, self.style);\n\n        switch (self.orientation) {\n            .vertical => {\n                var y = area.y;\n                while (y < area.bottom()) : (y += 1) {\n                    buf.set(area.x, y, track_cell);\n                }\n            },\n            .horizontal => {\n                var x = area.x;\n                while (x < area.right()) : (x += 1) {\n                    buf.set(x, area.y, track_cell);\n                }\n            },\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Draw the scrollbar thumb at the calculated position.\n    fn drawThumb(self: Scrollbar, area: Rect, start: u16, length: u16, buf: *Buffer) void {\n        if (length == 0) return;\n\n        const thumb_cell = Cell.styled(self.thumb_char, self.thumb_style);\n\n        switch (self.orientation) {\n            .vertical => {\n                const thumb_y = area.y +| start;\n                var y = thumb_y;\n                while (y < thumb_y +| length and y < area.bottom()) : (y += 1) {\n                    buf.set(area.x, y, thumb_cell);\n                }\n            },\n            .horizontal => {\n                const thumb_x = area.x +| start;\n                var x = thumb_x;\n                while (x < thumb_x +| length and x < area.right()) : (x += 1) {\n                    buf.set(x, area.y, thumb_cell);\n                }\n            },\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Calculate thumb position and size.\n    fn calculateThumb(self: Scrollbar, track_length: u16) struct { start: u16, length: u16 } {\n        if (self.total == 0 or self.viewport == 0 or track_length == 0) {\n            return .{ .start = 0, .length = 0 };\n        }\n\n        const total_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(self.total);\n        const viewport_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(self.viewport);\n        const track_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(track_length);\n        const position_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(self.position);\n\n        // Thumb length proportional to viewport/total ratio\n        const thumb_ratio = @min(viewport_f / total_f, 1.0);\n        var thumb_length: u16 = @intFromFloat(@max(thumb_ratio * track_f, 1.0));\n        thumb_length = @min(thumb_length, track_length);\n\n        // Thumb position based on scroll position\n        const scrollable_items = if (self.total > self.viewport)\n            self.total - self.viewport\n        else\n            0;\n\n        var thumb_start: u16 = 0;\n        if (scrollable_items > 0) {\n            const scrollable_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(scrollable_items);\n            const scrollable_track = track_length -| thumb_length;\n            const scrollable_track_f: f64 = @floatFromInt(scrollable_track);\n\n            const position_ratio = @min(position_f / scrollable_f, 1.0);\n            thumb_start = @intFromFloat(position_ratio * scrollable_track_f);\n        }\n\n        return .{ .start = thumb_start, .length = thumb_length };\n    }\n\n    /// Create a scrollbar for a list with the given state.\n    pub fn forList(items_count: usize, selected: usize, visible_rows: u16) Scrollbar {\n        return .{\n            .total = items_count,\n            .position = selected,\n            .viewport = visible_rows,\n        };\n    }\n};\n\n// ============================================================\n// SANITY TESTS - Basic Scrollbar functionality\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"sanity: Scrollbar with default values\" {\n    const scrollbar = Scrollbar{};\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), scrollbar.total);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), scrollbar.position);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 0), scrollbar.viewport);\n    try std.testing.expect(scrollbar.orientation == .vertical);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: Scrollbar with values\" {\n    const scrollbar = Scrollbar{\n        .total = 100,\n        .position = 25,\n        .viewport = 10,\n        .orientation = .horizontal,\n    };\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 100), scrollbar.total);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 25), scrollbar.position);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 10), scrollbar.viewport);\n    try std.testing.expect(scrollbar.orientation == .horizontal);\n}\n\ntest \"sanity: Scrollbar.forList creates correctly\" {\n std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 20), scrollbar.viewport);\n}\n\n// ============================================================\n// BEHAVIOR TESTS - Rendering\n// ============================================================\n\ntest \"behavior: Scrollbar renders vertical track\" {\n    var buf = try Buffer.init(std.testing.allocator, 10, 10);\n    defer state.\n   457/// Manages raw mode, alternate screen, and other terminal features.\n   458/// RAII pattern: deinit() restores terminal to original state.\n   459pub const Backend = struct {\n   460    /// File handle for terminal output.\n   461    handle: std.fs.File.Handle,\n   462    /// Original terminal state for restoration.\n   463    original_state: ?OriginalState,\n   464    /// Configuration used during initialization.\n   465    config: BackendConfig,\n   466    /// Whether the backend is currently active.\n   467    active: bool,\n   468    /// Detected terminal   } else struct {\n   475        termios: std.posix.termios,\n   476    };\n   477\n   478    /// Error type for backend operations.\n   479    pub const Error = error{\n   480        NotATty,\n   481        TerminalQueryFailed,\n   482        TerminalSetFailed,\n   483        IoError,\n   484    };\n   485\n   486    /// Initialize the terminal backend.\n   487    /// Enables raw mode and optional features based on config.\n   488    /// Registers panic handler to ensure cleanup on abnormal exit.\n   489    /// Returns error if stdout is not a TTY or terminal ops fail.\n   490    pub fn init(config: BackendConfig) Error!Backend {\n   491        if (is_windows) {\n   492            return initWindows(config);\n   493        } else {\n   494            return initPosix(config);\n   495        }\n   496    }\n   497\n   498    fn initPosix(config: BackendConfig) Error!Backend {\n   499        const fd = std.posix.STDOUT_FILENO;\n   500\n   501        if (!std.posix.isatty(fd)) {\n   502            return Error.NotATty;\n   503        }\n   504\n   505        // Detect terminal type and capabilities\n   506        const term_type = detectTerminalType();\n   507        const color_support = detectColorSupport();\n   508        const caps = TerminalCapabilities.fromTerminalType(term_type, color_support);\n   509\n   510        var self = Backend{\n   511            .handle = fd,\n   512            .original_state = null,\n   513            .config = config,\n   514            .active = false,\n   515            .capabilities = caps,\n   516        };\n   517\n   518        try self.enterRawMode();\n   519        self.active = true;\n   520\n   521        // Store state for emergency cleanup\n   522        if (self.original_state) |state| {\n   523            emergency_original_state = .{ .termios = state.termios };\n   524        }\n   525        emergency_config = config;\n   526        global_backend = &self;\n   527\n   528        if (config.alternate_screen and caps.alternate_screen) {\n   529            self.writeEscape(ENTER_ALTERNATE_SCREEN);\n   530        }\n   531\n   532        if (config.hide_cursor) {\n   533            self.writeEscape(HIDE_CURSOR);\n   534        }\n   535\n   536        if (config.mouse_capture and caps.mouse) {\n   537            self.enableMouse();\n   538        }\n   539\n   540        if (config.bracketed_paste and caps.bracketed_paste) {\n   541            self.writeEscape(ENABLE_BRACKETED_PASTE);\n   542        }\n   543\n   544        return self;\n   545    }\n   546\n   547    fn initWindows(config: BackendConfig) Error!Backend {\n   548        if (!is_windows) unreachable;\n   549\n   550        const stdout_handle = windows.GetStdHandle(windows.STD_OUTPUT_HANDLE) catch {\n   551            return Error.TerminalQueryFailed;\n   552        };\n   553        const stdin_handle = windows.GetStdHandle(windows.STD_INPUT_HANDLE) catch {\n   554            return Error.TerminalQueryFailed;\n   555        };\n   556\n   557        // Check if we're connected to a console\n   558        var mode: u32 = 0;\n   559        if (windows.kernel32.GetConsoleMode(stdout_handle, &mode) == 0) {\n   560            return Error.NotATty;\n   561        }\n   562\n   563        // Detect terminal type and capabilities\n   564        const term_type = detectTerminalType();\n   565        const color_support = detectColorSupport();\n   566        const caps = TerminalCapabilities.fromTerminalType(term_type, color_support);\n   567\n   568        // Save original console modes\n   569        var input_mode: u32 = 0;\n   570        _ = windows.kernel32.GetConsoleMode(stdin_handle, &input_mode);\n   571        var output_mode: u32 = 0;\n   572        _ = windows.kernel32.GetConsoleMode(stdout_handle, &output_mode);\n   573\n   574        var self = Backend{\n   575            .handle = stdout_handle,\n   576            .original_state = .{\n   577                .input_mode = input_mode,\n   578                .output_mode = output_mode,\n   579            },\n   580            .config = config,\n   581            .active = false,\n   582            .capabilities = caps,\n   583        };\n   584\n   585        // Enable virtual terminal processing for ANSI sequences\n   586        const ENABLE_VIRTUAL_TERMINAL_PROCESSING: u32 = 0x0004;\n   587        const DISABLE_NEWLINE_AUTO_RETURN: u32 = 0x0008;\n   588        const new_output_mode = output_mode | ENABLE_VIRTUAL_TERMINAL_PROCESSING | DISABLE_NEWLINE_AUTO_RETURN;\n   589        if (windows.kernel32.SetConsoleMode(stdout_handle, new_output_mode) == 0) {\n   590            return Error.TerminalSetFailed;\n   591        }\n   592\n   593        // Enable virtual terminal input processing\n   594        const ENABLE_VIRTUAL_TERMINAL_INPUT: u32 = 0x0200;\n   595        const ENABLE_WINDOW_INPUT: u32 = 0x0008;\n   596        var new_input_mode = input_mode | ENABLE_VIRTUAL_TERMINAL_INPUT | ENABLE_WINDOW_INPUT;\n   597        // Disable line input and echo for raw mode\n   598        const ENABLE_LINE_INPUT: u32 = 0x0002;\n   599        const ENABLE_ECHO_INPUT: u32 = 0x0004;\n   600        const ENABLE_PROCESSED_INPUT: u32 = 0x0001;\n   601        new_input_mode &= ~(ENABLE_LINE_INPUT | ENABLE_ECHO_INPUT | ENABLE_PROCESSED_INPUT);\n   602        if (windows.kernel32.SetConsoleMode(stdin_handle, new_input_mode) == 0) {\n   603            // Restore output mode on failure\n   604            _ = windows.kernel32.SetConsoleMode(stdout_handle, output_mode);\n   605            return Error.TerminalSetFailed;\n   606        }\n   607\n   608        self.active = true;\n   609\n   610        // Store state for emergency cleanup\n   611        emergency_original_state = .{\n   612            .input_mode = input_mode,\n   613            .output_mode = output_mode,\n   614        };\n   615        emergency_config = config;\n   616        global_backend = &self;\n   617\n   618        // Use ANSI escape sequences (works in Windows Terminal and modern Windows 10+)\n   619        if (config.alternate_screen and caps.alternate_screen) {\n   620            self.writeEscape(ENTER_ALTERNATE_SCREEN);\n   621        }\n   622\n   623        if (config.hide_cursor) {\n   624            self.writeEscape(HIDE_CURSOR);\n   625        }\n   626\n   627        if (config.mouse_capture and caps.mouse) {\n   628            self.enableMouse();\n   629        }\n   630\n   631        if (config.bracketed_paste and caps.bracketed_paste) {\n   632            self.writeEscape(ENABLE_BRACKETED_PASTE);\n   633        }\n   634\n   635        return self;\n   636    }\n   637\n   638    /// Restore terminal to original state.\n   639    /// Disables bracketed paste, mouse capture, shows cursor, leaves alternate screen,\n   640    /// and restores raw mode settings.\n   641    /// Safe to call multiple times.\n   642    pub fn deinit(self: *Backend) void {\n   643        if (!self.active) return;\n   644\n   645        // Disable bracketed paste\n   646        if (self.config.bracketed_paste and self.capabilities.bracketed_paste) {\n   647            self.writeEscape(DISABLE_BRACKETED_PASTE);\n   648        }\n   649\n   650        // Disable mouse capture\n   651        if (self.config.mouse_capture and self.capabilities.mouse) {\n   652            self.disableMouse();\n   653        }\n   654\n   655        // Show cursor\n   656        if (self.config.hide_cursor) {\n   657            self.writeEscape(SHOW_CURSOR);\n   658        }\n   659\n   660        // Leave alternate screen\n   661        if (self.config.alternate_screen and self.capabilities.alternate_screen) {\n   662            self.writeEscape(LEAVE_ALTERNATE_SCREEN);\n   663        }\n   664\n   665        // Restore terminal mode\n   666        if (is_windows) {\n   667            self.exitRawModeWindows();\n   668        } else {\n   669            self.exitRawMode();\n   670        }\n   671        self.active = false;\n   672\n   673        // Clear global state for panic handler\n   674        if (global_backend == self) {\n   675            global_backend = null;\n   676            emergency_original_state = null;\n   677            emergency_config = null;\n   678        }\n   679    }\n   680\n   681    /// Enter raw mode: disable line buffering, echo, and canonical mode.\n   682    fn enterRawMode(self: *Backend) Error!void {\n   683        if (is_windows) return; // Handled in initWindows\n   684\n   685        const original = std.posix.tcgetattr(self.handle) catch {\n   686            return Error.TerminalQueryFailed;\n   687        };\n   688        self.original_state = .{ .termios = original };\n   689\n   690        var raw = original;\n   691\n   692        // Input flags: disable break handling, CR-to-NL, parity, strip, flow control\n   693        raw.iflag.BRKINT = false;\n   694        raw.iflag.ICRNL = false;\n   695        raw.iflag.INPCK = false;\n   696        raw.iflag.ISTRIP = false;\n   697        raw.iflag.IXON = false;\n   698\n   699        // Output flags: disable post-processing\n   700        raw.oflag.OPOST = false;\n   701\n   702        // Control flags: set character size to 8 bits\n   703        raw.cflag.CSIZE = .CS8;\n   704\n   705        // Local flags: disable echo, canonical mode, signals, extended input\n   706        raw.lflag.ECHO = false;\n   707        raw.lflag.ICANON = false;\n   708        raw.lflag.ISIG = false;\n   709        raw.lflag.IEXTEN = false;\n   710\n   711        // Set minimum chars for non-canonical read\n   712        raw.cc[@intFromEnum(std.posix.V.MIN)] = 0;\n   713        raw.cc[@intFromEnum(std.posix.V.TIME)] = 1;\n   714\n   715        std.posix.tcsetattr(self.handle, .FLUSH, raw) catch {\n   716            return Error.TerminalSetFailed;\n   717        };\n   718    }\n   719\n   720    /// Exit raw mode: restore original terminal settings (POSIX).\n   721    fn exitRawMode(self: *Backend) void {\n   722        if (is_windows) return;\n   723        if (self.original_state) |state| {\n   724            std.posix.tcsetattr(self.handle, .FLUSH, state.termios) catch {};\n   725        }\n   726    }\n   727\n   728    /// Exit raw mode: restore original console modes (Windows).\n   729    fn exitRawModeWindows(self: *Backend) void {\n   730        if (!is_windows) return;\n   731        if (self.original_state) |state| {\n   732            const stdin_handle = windows.GetStdHandle(windows.STD_INPUT_HANDLE) catch return;\n   733            _ = windows.kernel32.SetConsoleMode(stdin_handle, state.input_mode);\n   734            _ = windows.kernel32.SetConsoleMode(self.handle, state.output_mode);\n   735        }\n   736    }\n   737\n   738    /// Enable mouse reporting (SGR mode for better coordinate handling).\n   739    fn enableMouse(self: *Backend) void {\n   740        if (self.capabilities.sgr_mouse) {\n   741            self.writeEscape(ENABLE_MOUSE_CAPTURE);\n   742            self.writeEscape(ENABLE_MOUSE_SGR);\n   743        } else if (self.capabilities.mouse) {\n   744            // Fall back to X10 mode for terminals without SGR support\n   745            self.writeEscape(ENABLE_MOUSE_CAPTURE);\n   746        }\n   747    }\n   748\n   749    /// Disable mouse reporting.\n   750    fn disableMouse(self: *Backend) void {\n   751        if (self.capabilities.sgr_mouse) {\n   752            self.writeEscape(DISABLE_MOUSE_SGR);\n   753        }\n   754        self.writeEscape(DISABLE_MOUSE_CAPTURE);\n   755    }\n   756\n   757    /// Write an escape sequence to the terminal.\n   758    fn writeEscape(self: *Backend, seq: []const u8) void {\n   759        const file = std.fs.File{ .handle = self.handle };\n   760        file.writeAll(seq) catch {};\n   761    }\n   762\n   763    /// Flush output to terminal.\n   764    pub fn flush(self: *Backend) void {\n   765        const file = std.fs.File{ .handle = self.handle };\n   766        file.sync() catch {};\n   767    }\n   768\n   769    /// Write bytes to the terminal.\n   770    pub fn write(self: *Backend, data: []const u8) Error!void {\n   771        const file = std.fs.File{ .handle = self.handle };\n   772        file.writeAll(data) catch {\n   773            return Error.IoError;\n   774        };\n   775    }\n   776\n   777    /// Move cursor to home position (0, 0).\n   778    pub fn cursorHome(self: *Backend) void {\n   779        self.writeEscape(CURSOR_HOME);\n   780    }\n   781\n   782    /// Move cursor to specific position (0-indexed).\n   783    pub fn cursorTo(self: *Backend, x: u16, y: u16) void {\n   784        var buf: [32]u8 = undefined;\n   785        const seq = std.fmt.bufPrint(&buf, \"\\x1b[{d};{d}H\", .{ y + 1, x + 1 }) catch return;\n   786        self.writeEscape(seq);\n   787    }\n   788\n   789    /// Clear the entire screen.\n   790    pub fn clearScreen(self: *Backend) void {\n   791        self.writeEscape(CLEAR_SCREEN);\n   792    }\n   793\n   794    /// Get terminal size (width, height).\n   795    pub fn getSize(self: *Backend) TerminalSize {\n   796        if (is_windows) {\n   797            return getSizeWindows(self.handle);\n   798        } else {\n   799            return getSizeForFd(self.handle);\n   800        }\n   801    }\n   802\n   803    /// Get detected terminal capabilities.\n   804    pub fn getCapabilities(self: *Backend) TerminalCapabilities {\n   805        return self.capabilities;\n   806    }\n   807\n   808    /// Detect terminal color support level.\n   809    /// Checks environment variables COLORTERM and TERM to determine capability.\n   810    /// Returns the highest detected color support level.\n   811    pub fn getColorSupport(self: *Backend) ColorSupport {\n   812        return self.capabilities.color_support;\n   813    }\n   814\n   815    // ANSI escape sequences\n   816    pub const ENTER_ALTERNATE_SCREEN = \"\\x1b[?1049h\";\n   817    pub const LEAVE_ALTERNATE_SCREEN = \"\\x1b[?1049l\";\n   818    pub const HIDE_CURSOR = \"\\x1b[?25l\";\n   819    pub const SHOW_CURSOR = \"\\x1b[?25h\";\n   820    pub const CLEAR_SCREEN = \"\\x1b[2J\";\n   821    pub const CURSOR_HOME = \"\\x1b[H\";\n   822\n   823    pub const ENABLE_MOUSE_CAPTURE = \"\\x1b[?1000h\\x1b[?1002h\\x1b[?1003h\";\n   824    pub const DISABLE_MOUSE_CAPTURE = \"\\x1b[?1003l\\x1b[?1002l\\x1b[?1000l\";\n   825    pub const ENABLE_MOUSE_SGR = \"\\x1b[?1006h\";\n   826    pub const DISABLE_MOUSE_SGR = \"\\x1b[?1006l\";\n   827\n   828    pub const ENABLE_BRACKETED_PASTE = \"\\x1b[?2004h\";\n   829    pub const DISABLE_BRACKETED_PASTE = \"\\x1b[?2004l\";\n   830};\n   831\n   832// ============================================================\n   833// TERMINAL DETECTION\n   834// ============================================================\n   835\n   836/// Detect the terminal type from environment variables.\n   837pub fn detectTerminalType() TerminalType {\n   838    if (is_windows) {\n   839        return detectTerminalTypeWindows();\n   840    } else {\n   841        return detectTerminalTypePosix();\n   842    }\n   843}\n   844\n   845fn detectTerminalTypePosix() TerminalType {\n   846    // Check for specific terminal indicators\n   847\n   848    // iTerm2\n   849    if (getEnv(\"ITERM_SESSION_ID\") != null or getEnv(\"ITERM_PROFILE\") != null) {\n   850        return .iterm2;\n   851    }\n   852\n   853    // Kitty\n   854    if (getEnv(\"KITTY_WINDOW_ID\") != null) {\n   855        return .kitty;\n   856    }\n   857\n   858    // WezTerm\n   859    if (getEnv(\"WEZTERM_PANE\") != null or getEnv(\"WEZTERM_UNIX_SOCKET\") != null) {\n   860        return .wezterm;\n   861    }\n   862\n   863    // Alacritty (check TERM first, then ALACRITTY_LOG)\n   864    if (getEnv(\"ALACRITTY_LOG\") != null or getEnv(\"ALACRITTY_SOCKET\") != null) {\n   865        return .alacritty;\n   866    }\n   867\n   868    // Konsole\n   869    if (getEnv(\"KONSOLE_VERSION\") != null) {\n   870        return .konsole;\n   871    }\n   872\n   873    // GNOME Terminal / VTE\n   874    if (getEnv(\"VTE_VERSION\") != null or getEnv(\"GNOME_TERMINAL_SCREEN\") != null) {\n   875        return .gnome_terminal;\n   876    }\n   877\n   878    // Check TERM_PROGRAM\n   879    if (getEnv(\"TERM_PROGRAM\")) |term_program| {\n   880        if (std.mem.eql(u8, term_program, \"iTerm.app\")) return .iterm2;\n   881        if (std.mem.eql(u8, term_program, \"Apple_Terminal\")) return .xterm;\n   882        if (std.mem.eql(u8, term_program, \"WezTerm\")) return .wezterm;\n   883        if (std.mem.eql(u8, term_program, \"Hyper\")) return .xterm;\n   884        if (std.mem.eql(u8, term_program, \"vscode\")) return .xterm;\n   885    }\n   886\n   887    // tmux\n   888    if (getEnv(\"TMUX\") != null) {\n   889        return .tmux;\n   890    }\n   891\n   892    // GNU Screen\n   893    if (getEnv(\"STY\") != null) {\n   894        return .screen;\n   895    }\n   896\n   897    // Check TERM variable\n   898    if (getEnv(\"TERM\")) |term| {\n   899        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"alacritty\")) return .alacritty;\n   900        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"kitty\")) return .kitty;\n   901        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"xterm\")) return .xterm;\n   902        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"rxvt\")) return .rxvt;\n   903        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"screen\")) return .screen;\n   904        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"tmux\")) return .tmux;\n   905        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"linux\")) return .linux_console;\n   906        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"vte\")) return .gnome_terminal;\n   907        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"gnome\")) return .gnome_terminal;\n   908        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"konsole\")) return .konsole;\n   909    }\n   910\n   911    return .unknown;\n   912}\n   913\n   914fn detectTerminalTypeWindows() TerminalType {\n   915    if (!is_windows) return .unknown;\n   916\n   917    // Check for Windows Terminal\n   918    if (getEnv(\"WT_SESSION\") != null or getEnv(\"WT_PROFILE_ID\") != null) {\n   919        return .windows_terminal;\n   920    }\n   921\n   922    // Check for ConEmu\n   923    if (getEnv(\"ConEmuPID\") != null or getEnv(\"ConEmuANSI\") != null) {\n   924        return .conemu;\n   925    }\n   926\n   927    // Check for various terminal emulators that might run on Windows\n   928    if (getEnv(\"TERM_PROGRAM\")) |term_program| {\n   929        if (std.mem.eql(u8, term_program, \"mintty\")) return .xterm;\n   930        if (std.mem.eql(u8, term_program, \"vscode\")) return .xterm;\n   931        if (std.mem.eql(u8, term_program, \"Hyper\")) return .xterm;\n   932        if (std.mem.eql(u8, term_program, \"Alacritty\")) return .alacritty;\n   933        if (std.mem.eql(u8, term_program, \"WezTerm\")) return .wezterm;\n   934    }\n   935\n   936    // Check TERM for MSYS/Cygwin/Git Bash\n   937    if (getEnv(\"TERM\")) |term| {\n   938        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"xterm\")) return .xterm;\n   939        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"cygwin\")) return .xterm;\n   940        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"mintty\")) return .xterm;\n   941    }\n   942\n   943    // Check for MSYSTEM (Git Bash / MSYS2)\n   944    if (getEnv(\"MSYSTEM\") != null) {\n   945        return .xterm;\n   946    }\n   947\n   948    // Default to cmd.exe for legacy Windows console\n   949    return .cmd_exe;\n   950}\n   951\n   952/// Detect terminal color support from environment variables.\n   953/// This is a standalone function that doesn't require a Backend instance.\n   954/// Checks COLORTERM and TERM environment variables to determine capability.\n   955pub fn detectColorSupport() ColorSupport {\n   956    if (is_windows) {\n   957        return detectColorSupportWindows();\n   958    } else {\n   959        return detectColorSupportPosix();\n   960    }\n   961}\n   962\n   963fn detectColorSupportPosix() ColorSupport {\n   964    // Check COLORTERM first - most reliable indicator of true color\n   965    if (getEnv(\"COLORTERM\")) |colorterm| {\n   966        if (std.mem.eql(u8, colorterm, \"truecolor\") or std.mem.eql(u8, colorterm, \"24bit\")) {\n   967            return .true_color;\n   968        }\n   969    }\n   970\n   971    // Check for specific terminal environment variables that indicate true color\n   972    // iTerm2\n   973    if (getEnv(\"ITERM_SESSION_ID\") != null) return .true_color;\n   974    // Kitty\n   975    if (getEnv(\"KITTY_WINDOW_ID\") != null) return .true_color;\n   976    // WezTerm\n   977    if (getEnv(\"WEZTERM_PANE\") != null) return .true_color;\n   978    // Alacritty (via socket or log)\n   979    if (getEnv(\"ALACRITTY_LOG\") != null or getEnv(\"ALACRITTY_SOCKET\") != null) return .true_color;\n   980    // Konsole (version 220000+ has true color)\n   981    if (getEnv(\"KONSOLE_VERSION\") != null) return .true_color;\n   982    // VTE 3600+ has true color (GNOME Terminal)\n   983    if (getEnv(\"VTE_VERSION\") != null) return .true_color;\n   984\n   985    // Check TERM for terminal type hints\n   986    if (getEnv(\"TERM\")) |term| {\n   987        // True color indicators in TERM\n   988        if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, term, \"truecolor\") != null or\n   989            std.mem.indexOf(u8, term, \"24bit\") != null or\n   990            std.mem.indexOf(u8, term, \"direct\") != null)\n   991        {\n   992            return .true_color;\n   993        }\n   994\n   995        // Known terminals that support true color\n   996        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"alacritty\") or\n   997            std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"kitty\"))\n   998        {\n   999            return .true_color;\n  1000        }\n  1001\n  1002        // 256 color indicators\n  1003        if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, term, \"256color\") != null or\n  1004            std.mem.indexOf(u8, term, \"256\") != null)\n  1005        {\n  1006            return .extended;\n  1007        }\n  1008\n  1009        // Known modern terminals that typically support at least 256 colors\n  1010        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"xterm\") or\n  1011            std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"screen\") or\n  1012            std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"tmux\") or\n  1013            std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"vte\") or\n  1014            std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"gnome\") or\n  1015            std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"konsole\") or\n  1016            std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"rxvt\"))\n  1017        {\n  1018            return .extended;\n  1019        }\n  1020\n  1021        // Linux console is limited\n  1022        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"linux\")) {\n  1023            return .basic;\n  1024        }\n  1025    }\n  1026\n  1027    // Default to basic 16-color support\n  1028    return .basic;\n  1029}\n  1030\n  1031fn detectColorSupportWindows() ColorSupport {\n  1032    if (!is_windows) return .basic;\n  1033\n  1034    // Windows Terminal supports true color\n  1035    if (getEnv(\"WT_SESSION\") != null or getEnv(\"WT_PROFILE_ID\") != null) {\n  1036        return .true_color;\n  1037    }\n  1038\n  1039    // ConEmu with ANSI support\n  1040    if (getEnv(\"ConEmuANSI\")) |ansi| {\n  1041        if (std.mem.eql(u8, ansi, \"ON\")) {\n  1042            return .true_color;\n  1043        }\n  1044    }\n  1045\n  1046    // Check COLORTERM (might be set by some terminals)\n  1047    if (getEnv(\"COLORTERM\")) |colorterm| {\n  1048        if (std.mem.eql(u8, colorterm, \"truecolor\") or std.mem.eql(u8, colorterm, \"24bit\")) {\n  1049            return .true_color;\n  1050        }\n  1051    }\n  1052\n  1053    // Check for terminal emulators running on Windows\n  1054    if (getEnv(\"TERM_PROGRAM\")) |term_program| {\n  1055        if (std.mem.eql(u8, term_program, \"Alacritty\") or\n  1056            std.mem.eql(u8, term_program, \"WezTerm\") or\n  1057            std.mem.eql(u8, term_program, \"mintty\"))\n  1058        {\n  1059            return .true_color;\n  1060        }\n  1061        if (std.mem.eql(u8, term_program, \"vscode\")) {\n  1062            return .extended;\n  1063        }\n  1064    }\n  1065\n  1066    // MSYS2/Git Bash typically support 256 colors\n  1067    if (getEnv(\"MSYSTEM\") != null) {\n  1068        return .extended;\n  1069    }\n  1070\n  1071    // Check TERM for hints\n  1072    if (getEnv(\"TERM\")) |term| {\n  1073        if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, term, \"256color\") != null) {\n  1074            return .extended;\n  1075        }\n  1076        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"xterm\") or\n  1077            std.mem.startsWith(u8, term, \"mintty\"))\n  1078        {\n  1079            return .extended;\n  1080        }\n  1081    }\n  1082\n  1083    // Modern Windows 10+ console supports 256 colors and possibly true color\n  1084    // but we're conservative here - default to extended\n  1085    return .extended;\n  1086}\n  1087\n  1088/// Cross-platform environment variable getter.\n  1089fn getEnv(name: []const u8) ?[]const u8 {\n  1090    if (is_windows) {\n  1091        return std.process.getEnvVarOwned(std.heap.page_allocator, name) catch null;\n  1092    } else {\n  1093        return std.posix.getenv(name);\n  1094    }\n  1095}\n  1096\n  1097/// Internal: get terminal size for a specific file descriptor (POSIX).\n  1098fn getSizeForFd(fd: std.posix.fd_t) TerminalSize {\n  1099    var ws: std.posix.winsize = undefined;\n  1100    const result = std.posix.system.ioctl(fd, std.posix.T.IOCGWINSZ, @intFromPtr(&ws));\n  1101    if (result == 0) {\n  1102        return .{ .width = ws.col, .height = ws.row };\n  1103    }\n  1104    return .{ .width = 80, .height = 24 };\n  1105}\n  1106\n  1107/// Internal: get terminal size (Windows).\n  1108fn getSizeWindows(handle: std.fs.File.Handle) TerminalSize {\n  1109    if (!is_windows) return .{ .width = 80, .height = 24 };\n  1110\n  1111    var csbi: windows.CONSOLE_SCREEN_BUFFER_INFO = undefined;\n  1112    if (windows.kernel32.GetConsoleScreenBufferInfo(handle, &csbi) != 0) {\n  1113        const width = csbi.srWindow.Right - csbi.srWindow.Left + 1;\n  1114        const height = csbi.srWindow.Bottom - csbi.srWindow.Top + 1;\n  1115        return .{\n  1116            .width = @intCast(@max(1, width)),\n  1117            .height = @intCast(@max(1, height)),\n  1118        };\n  1119    }\n  1120    return .{ .width = 80, .height = 24 };\n  1121}\n  1122\n  1123/// Get terminal size without requiring a Backend instance.\n  1124/// Useful for initial configuration before Backend initialization.\n  1125/// Returns default 80x24 if size cannot be determined.\n  1126pub fn getTerminalSize() TerminalSize {\n  1127    if (is_windows) {\n  1128        const stdout_handle = windows.GetStdHandle(windows.STD_OUTPUT_HANDLE) catch {\n  1129            return .{ .width = 80, .height = 24 };\n  1130        };\n  1131        return getSizeWindows(stdout_handle);\n  1132    } else {\n  1133        return getSizeForFd(std.posix.STDOUT_FILENO);\n  1134    }\n  1135}\n  1136\n  1137// ============================================================\n  1138// BUFFERED OUTPUT\n  1139// ============================================================\n  1140\n  1141/// Buffered terminal output with rich_zig integration.\n  1142/// Accumulates output in a buffer and flushes to the terminal efficiently.\n  1143/// Provides cursor positioning, clearing, and styled text output.\n  1144pub fn Output(comptime buffer_size: usize) type {\n  1145    return struct {\n  1146        const Self = @This();\n  1147\n  1148        /// Internal buffer for accumulating output.\n  1149        buffer: [buffer_size]u8 = undefined,\n  1150        /// Current position in the buffer.\n  1151        pos: usize = 0,\n  1152        /// File handle for output.\n  1153        handle: std.fs.File.Handle,\n  1154        /// Detected color system for ANSI rendering.\n  1155        color_system: ColorSystem,\n  1156        /// Last style written (for optimization).\n  1157        last_style: ?Style = null,\n  1158\n  1159        /// Initialize output with detected color support.\n  1160        pub fn init(handle: std.fs.File.Handle) Self {\n  1161            return .{\n  1162                .handle = handle,\n  1163                .color_system = colorSupportToSystem(detectColorSupport()),\n  1164            };\n  1165        }\n  1166\n  1167        /// Initialize output with explicit color system.\n  1168        pub fn initWithColorSystem(handle: std.fs.File.Handle, color_system: ColorSystem) Self {\n  1169            return .{\n  1170                .handle = handle,\n  1171                .color_system = color_system,\n  1172            };\n  1173        }\n  1174\n  1175        /// Write raw bytes to the buffer.\n  1176        pub fn writeRaw(self: *Self, data: []const u8) void {\n  1177            for (data) |byte| {\n  1178                if (self.pos >= buffer_size) {\n  1179                    self.flushInternal();\n  1180                }\n  1181                self.buffer[self.pos] = byte;\n  1182                self.pos += 1;\n  1183            }\n  1184        }\n  1185\n  1186        /// Write a single byte to the buffer.\n  1187        pub fn writeByte(self: *Self, byte: u8) void {\n  1188            if (self.pos >= buffer_size) {\n  1189                self.flushInternal();\n  1190            }\n  1191            self.buffer[self.pos] = byte;\n  1192            self.pos += 1;\n  1193        }\n  1194\n  1195        /// Get a writer interface for use with std.fmt.\n  1196        pub fn writer(self: *Self) std.io.GenericWriter(*Self, error{}, writeFn) {\n  1197            return .{ .context = self };\n  1198        }\n  1199\n  1200        fn writeFn(self: *Self, data: []const u8) error{}!usize {\n  1201            self.writeRaw(data);\n  1202            return data.len;\n  1203        }\n  1204\n  1205        /// Move cursor to home position (0, 0).\n  1206        pub fn cursorHome(self: *Self) void {\n  1207            self.writeRaw(\"\\x1b[H\");\n  1208        }\n  1209\n  1210        /// Move cursor to specific position (0-indexed).\n  1211        pub fn cursorTo(self: *Self, x: u16, y: u16) void {\n  1212            var buf: [32]u8 = undefined;\n  1213            const seq = std.fmt.bufPrint(&buf, \"\\x1b[{d};{d}H\", .{ y + 1, x + 1 }) catch return;\n  1214            self.writeRaw(seq);\n  1215        }\n  1216\n  1217        /// Move cursor up by n rows.\n  1218        pub fn cursorUp(self: *Self, n: u16) void {\n  1219            if (n == 0) return;\n  1220            var buf: [16]u8 = undefined;\n  1221            const seq = std.fmt.bufPrint(&buf, \"\\x1b[{d}A\", .{n}) catch return;\n  1222            self.writeRaw(seq);\n  1223        }\n  1224\n  1225        /// Move cursor down by n rows.\n  1226        pub fn cursorDown(self: *Self, n: u16) void {\n  1227            if (n == 0) return;\n  1228            var buf: [16]u8 = undefined;\n  1229            const seq = std.fmt.bufPrint(&buf, \"\\x1b[{d}B\", .{n}) catch return;\n  1230            self.writeRaw(seq);\n  1231        }\n  1232\n  1233        /// Move cursor forward by n columns.\n  1234        pub fn cursorForward(self: *Self, n: u16) void {\n  1235            if (n == 0) return;\n  1236            var buf: [16]u8 = undefined;\n  1237            const seq = std.fmt.bufPrint(&buf, \"\\x1b[{d}C\", .{n}) catch return;\n  1238            self.writeRaw(seq);\n  1239        }\n  1240\n  1241        /// Move cursor backward by n columns.\n  1242        pub fn cursorBackward(self: *Self, n: u16) void {\n  1243            if (n == 0) return;\n  1244            var buf: [16]u8 = undefined;\n  1245            const seq = std.fmt.bufPrint(&buf, \"\\x1b[{d}D\", .{n}) catch return;\n  1246            self.writeRaw(seq);\n  1247        }\n  1248\n  1249        /// Clear the entire screen.\n  1250        pub fn clearScreen(self: *Self) void {\n  1251            self.writeRaw(\"\\x1b[2J\");\n  1252        }\n  1253\n  1254        /// Clear from cursor to end of screen.\n  1255        pub fn clearToEndOfScreen(self: *Self) void {\n  1256            self.writeRaw(\"\\x1b[0J\");\n  1257        }\n  1258\n  1259        /// Clear from cursor to start of screen.\n  1260        pub fn clearToStartOfScreen(self: *Self) void {\n  1261            self.writeRaw(\"\\x1b[1J\");\n  1262        }\n  1263\n  1264        /// Clear the current line.\n  1265        pub fn clearLine(self: *Self) void {\n  1266            self.writeRaw(\"\\x1b[2K\");\n  1267        }\n  1268\n  1269        /// Clear from cursor to end of line.\n  1270        pub fn clearToEndOfLine(self: *Self) void {\n  1271            self.writeRaw(\"\\x1b[0K\");\n  1272        }\n  1273\n  1274        /// Clear from cursor to start of line.\n  1275        pub fn clearToStartOfLine(self: *Self) void {\n  1276            self.writeRaw(\"\\x1b[1K\");\n  1277        }\n  1278\n  1279        /// Show the cursor.\n  1280        pub fn showCursor(self: *Self) void {\n  1281            self.writeRaw(\"\\x1b[?25h\");\n  1282        }\n  1283\n  1284        /// Hide the cursor.\n  1285        pub fn hideCursor(self: *Self) void {\n  1286            self.writeRaw(\"\\x1b[?25l\");\n  1287        }\n  1288\n  1289        /// Set the text style using rich_zig ANSI rendering.\n  1290        pub fn setStyle(self: *Self, style: Style) void {\n  1291            // Skip if same as last style\n  1292            if (self.last_style) |last| {\n  1293                if (last.eql(style)) return;\n  1294            }\n  1295\n  1296            style.renderAnsi(self.color_system, self.writer()) catch {};\n  1297            self.last_style = style;\n  1298        }\n  1299\n  1300        /// Reset to default style.\n  1301        pub fn resetStyle(self: *Self) void {\n  1302            self.writeRaw(\"\\x1b[0m\");\n  1303            self.last_style = null;\n  1304        }\n  1305\n  1306        /// Write styled text (sets style, writes text, does not reset).\n  1307        pub fn writeStyled(self: *Self, text: []const u8, style: Style) void {\n  1308            if (!style.isEmpty()) {\n  1309                self.setStyle(style);\n  1310            }\n  1311            self.writeRaw(text);\n  1312        }\n  1313\n  1314        /// Write a character with the given style.\n  1315        pub fn writeChar(self: *Self, char: u21, style: Style) void {\n  1316            if (!style.isEmpty()) {\n  1317                self.setStyle(style);\n  1318            }\n  1319            var utf8_buf: [4]u8 = undefined;\n  1320            const len = std.unicode.utf8Encode(char, &utf8_buf) catch 1;\n  1321            self.writeRaw(utf8_buf[0..len]);\n  1322        }\n  1323\n  1324        /// Write a segment (styled text span from rich_zig).\n  1325        pub fn writeSegment(self: *Self, segment: Segment) void {\n  1326            segment.render(self.writer(), self.color_system) catch {};\n  1327        }\n  1328\n  1329        /// Execute a control code.\n  1330        pub fn writeControl(self: *Self, control: ControlCode) void {\n  1331            control.toEscapeSequence(self.writer()) catch {};\n  1332        }\n  1333\n  1334        /// Flush buffered output to the terminal.\n  1335        pub fn flush(self: *Self) void {\n  1336            self.flushInternal();\n  1337        }\n  1338\n  1339        fn flushInternal(self: *Self) void {\n  1340            if (self.pos == 0) return;\n  1341            const file = std.fs.File{ .handle = self.handle };\n  1342            file.writeAll(self.buffer[0..self.pos]) catch {};\n  1343            self.pos = 0;\n  1344        }\n  1345\n  1346        /// Get remaining buffer capacity.\n  1347        pub fn remaining(self: Self) usize {\n  1348            return buffer_size - self.pos;\n  1349        }\n  1350\n  1351        /// Check if buffer is empty.\n  1352        pub fn isEmpty(self: Self) bool {\n  1353            return self.pos == 0;\n  1354        }\n  1355    };\n  1356}\n  1357\n  1358/// Default output type with 8KB buffer.\n  1359pub const DefaultOutput = Output(8192);\n  1360\n  1361/// Convert ColorSupport enum to rich_zig's ColorSystem.\n  1362pub fn colorSupportToSystem(support: ColorSupport) ColorSystem {\n  1363    return switch (support) {\n  1364        .basic => .standard,\n  1365        .extended => .eight_bit,\n  1366        .true_color => .truecolor,\n  1367    };\n  1368}\n  1369\n  1370// ============================================================\n  1371// SANITY TESTS -
